After cauterize on the figure that you have signed little and little many times, so that the cure is burned at the place; and the sign of the work of health is that you see the paper retreat, and the hairs rise to the point where the oil is; then raise your hand, and leave it like this for III days, then I put cotton wet in the butter as much as the healing is done; after the cure of the wound as long as it is healthy.
Et se aprés ceu vienent li poilz, et li papiere est mollifie adonques rencomence le cautere sus cel leu meisme, si com tu as fait premiers; et se li poil sont defuer, si le cauterize tant que li papiere soit levee a son leu natureil, et soit igals, et ne poignent mie li poil l’oil.	And if after that come the hairs, and the paper is softened then start again the cautery on that middle height, as you did first; and if the hairs are gone, cauterize until the paper comes back to its natural height, and is even, and do not touch the hair with oil.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il laisse les poilz tant qu’il soient grans et igalz, puis fai de parchemin la forme de la foille de mirte; puis pren de savon fransois et de vive chalz, de chescun une .З., et broie ensamble bien; et le fai hastanment, si qu’il ne refroide, puis en espant sus la forme que tu es fait sicom la foille dou mirte, et met sus la papiere des eulz; et se li maladie tient en I oil soulement, si doit on ovrer en I, et se en ambedous ausi; et met desoz l’oil coton moilliet en abin d’uef; et li chiés dou malaide soit en ton sain et met ton doi mostrant sus la medicine, et presse I poc et lou muef toutes les fois que li malaide sent mordication de la medicine, car il sent mordication ausi com de feu.	And if after that come the hairs, and the paper is softened then start again the fire cautery on that middle height, as you did first; and if the hairs are gone, cauterize until the paper comes back to its natural height, and is even, and do not touch the hair with oil. The medicine fire cautery is that you command the patient to let the hairs grow long and even, then make of parchment the shape of the bay leaf; then take of French soap and hot water, of each a .Z., and grind them together well; and do it hurriedly, so that it does not cool down, then apply to the shape you have made like the bay leaf leaf, and put on the paper the hairs; and if the disease is only in the oil, then should be used also in the water; and put away the cotton oil moistened in the bowl of urine; and the patient's joint be in your hand and place your thumb showing towards the medicine, and press it little by little every time the patient feels tingling from the medicine, for he feels tingling also like fire.
Quant tu as ceu fait longement, si oste la medicine a ton doit.	As you have done for so long, if the medicine sticks to your tongue.
Et quant li mordication sera passee, si leve le leu d’awe, et rewarde se tu vois la papiere levee ausi com s’ele estoit levee par constraignement de feu ou par incision; et s’il est ensi, si est bien.	And when the blister has passed, if the wound is raised up, and you see the paper raised as if it had been raised by fire or by an incision; and if so, then it is well.
Se ceu non, si remet encor de la medicine sus lou leu ou li medicine n’ait ovreit, tant que tes ovraiges soit igalz, et tes eulz mis a point; puis met sus coton moilliet en burre tant que li keurs ars soit cheus, aprés cure le leu de l’oignement qui est apelez «dyafenis» et d’autre, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If not, put the medicine back on the place where the medicine has not worked, as long as your blisters are even and your hairs are in order; then put cotton wet with burre on it as long as the burn is sore, after treating the wounded place which is called 'dyafenis' and other things, as long as it is healed.
Et se t’est mestier que tu te warde bien a ton ovraige par grant warde qu’il ne chiece point de la medicine as eulz.	And if you must guard your wound well, by great care so that it does not break out with the medicine's hairs.
Et se li papiere devient mole aprés, et li poil poignent en l’oil, si recomence la medicine sus celui leu qui est mollifiez de la papiere proprement, ensi com tu as fait devant; aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez; et c’est li forme de la fuelle dou mirte:	And if the paper becomes soft again, and the hairs stick in the oil, then repeat the medicine on that place which is made soft by the paper properly, as you have done before; after treating it until it is healed; and this is the form of the wound of the foot:
Et saichés que li eul des homes sont divers en grandor et en petitece, et selonc ceu soit tes constraignemens; et ne soit mie reponue li droite voie a celui cui est li estude de cest art.	And know that the eyes of men are different in size and shape, and according to what is required; and do not answer the right way to those for whom this study is.
de la cure de fistule par cautere	For the cure of a fistula by cauterization:
Quant tu cures fistule si com nos avons dit en divisions des maladies, et tes cures ne profitent mie, adonques covient il que tu li fais cautere selonc ceste maniere.	When you treat a fistula as we have said in the division of diseases, and your treatments do not benefit, then it is necessary to apply cauterization according to this method.
Comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain; et teigne li menistres son chief entre tes mains en teil maniere qu’il ne se mueve, ne ne demoinne son chief; aprés met coton moilliet en abin d’uef ou en jus de persillion sus l’oil; aprés chaufe le cautere qui est teilz: et est chevez au chief si com li forme d’une penne de vouteul, ensamble la queil soit li cautere; se tu vues, si soit apointé des l’un chief dusc’a l’autre, et se tu vues, si soit ausi com une tente; mais toutevoie, cist qui est chevez vaut mues por ton ovraige.	Instruct the patient to place their hair in your care; and dip the hairs between your hands in a bowl of warm oil or juice of pears, then heat the cauterizer as follows: and apply it to the hair at the base like a feather, together with the tip of the cauterizer; if you see, if is applied from one side of the head to the other, and if you do not see, it should be applied like a tent; but in any case, the hair that is heated serves for your work.
Aprés presse la fistule s’ele est overte, et en trai la porriture, et la seche; et s’ele est close, si la oevre, et trai fuers la bowe; aprés met sus le cautere chaut forment, et tien ta main au cautere a la partie dou neif ensus de l’oil, que ta mains ne faice folie; et met le cautere en la graisse de l’oil, et la corromp.	After pressing the fistula is opened, and treat it with poultices, and dry it up; and if it closes, then treat it with heat, and firmly hold the cautery to the part below the oil behind the ear, so that your hands do not go wild; and place the cautery in the fat of the oil, and corrupt it.
Se tu viens au comencement dou cautere jusc’a l’os, si serait bien.	If you come to the cauterization just to the bone, it would be good.
Se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere encor une fois, et autre se tu en as mestier, et le laisse III jors; aprés i met sus coton moilliet en burre, et lou cure de l’oignement desiccatif tant qu’il soit sanez, et se XL jors passent qu’il ne soit sanez, si met sus medicine ague corrosive tant que li os soit descovers; et lou reis selonc ceu que il venrait en son chapistre.	If not, then start cauterizing again, and if you need to do it more, and leave it for three days; after that, put cotton wet with butter on it, and treat with a drying medicine until it is healthy, and if forty days pass and it is not healthy, then put on a corrosive medicine until the bone is uncovered; and treat according to this that came in his chapter.
Et i a une maniere de cautere de fistule que aucun des anciens dirent.	And I have a way of cauterizing fistulas, which no one of the ancients mentioned.
Entens a fistule, et fens le leu; aprés met en la fendure I camahan subtil de coi ci est li forme:	Understand a fistula, and seal the spot; then, put in the thin layer of caugh which is the shape:
et i font a la quantiteit d’une .З. de plonc; et tien ta main ou camahan fermement, et ne se mueve li malaides nes point, que li plons fondus ne corre a son oil; et covient c’on mette sus l’oil a malaide coton moilliet en abin d’uefz ou en awe: li plonc si art lou leu de fistule, et lou saine per mervillouse saniteit.	And I make it in the quantity of half an inch of plaster; and hold your hand firmly, so that the plaster does not move at all, so that the melted plaster does not run to its oil; and you must put cotton wool wet with ointment on a piece of cloth or a napkin: the plaster, if it is made in this way, will enter into the fistula, and will heal with a wonderful cure.
Et se li fistule est sanee per le cautere que nos avons dit, c’est boin.	And if the fistula is healed by the cauterization that we have spoken of, it is good.
Se ce non, si covient aministrer pertus au neif, et ramener la fistule au cors dou neif selonc ceu qu’il covient en som propre leu.	But if not, then it is necessary to give a pound to the nose, and to bring back the fistula to the root of the nose according to what one should do in his own place.
des crevaices en levres	crevasses on lips
Mout de fois avienent crevaices en levres que sont apelees «poil», et meismement en levres des enfans.	The mouth sometimes causes crevices in the lips, which are called "hair," and sometimes in the lips of children.
Quant tu cures ces crevaices de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et li cure ne profite, adonques eschaufe I petit cautere cultellaire selonc ceste forme:	When you treat these crevices as we have said in the divisions, and the cure does not benefit, then a small surgical cauterization is performed according to this form:
Et le met hastanment en celles crevaices tant qu’il viegne jusc’a font; aprés cure le leu de cerote tant qu’il soit sanez.	And place thereon a small patch of burn as soon as it comes; after the burn, place a poultice until it is healthy.
de l’aposteme de la goule	of the abscess from the throat
Quant apostume vient en la racine de la goule ou en l’uve, ou ou palais, ou as racines des dens, aprés fait porriture et ront et est enveillis et devient fistule; et tu le cures si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie: adonques covient il que tu aies I cautere selonc la quantiteit de la fistule; aprés le bote ou pertus de la fistule, et tien ta main tant que li fer chaus viegne au font de li, et ou derrien leu; et fai ensi une fois ou II, aprés le cure de ce que nos avons dit en cures, tant qu’il soit sanez; et s’il est curez ensi, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si covient descovrir le leu et oster l’os corrumput, selonc ceu que vos le troverez en son chapistre.	When the abscess comes at the root of the throat or the palate or the roots of the teeth, after having made a poultice and left it until it is soft and has become an ulcer; and you treat it as we have said in the divisions, but it does not benefit: then you must take a cauterization according to the quantity of the ulcer; after having boiled the hole or hole of the ulcer, and keeping your hand there until the iron comes up to the font of it, and applying it thus once or twice, after the cure as we have said, until it is healthy; and if it is cured thus, it is good; and if not, you must discover the place and remove the rotten bone, according to what you will find in its chapter.
dou movement des dens	dou movement des dens
Quant les gencives sont mollifies par moistor et les dens muevent, et tu le cures per medicines et ceu ne vaut, adonc met le chief dou malaide en ton sain; aprés eschaufe le cautere dont li forme venra ci aprés en teil maniere que tu mettes une cainne sor le dent; et met dedens le cautere chaut hastanment, et tien tant ta main que li malaides sente la chalor venant a la racine dou dent; aprés lieve ta main et rencomence le cautere selonc ta volenteit; aprés emplisse li malaides sa bouche d’awe salee, et la teigne une houre et raiche fuers.	If the gums are softened by moisture and the teeth move, and you can't fix it with medicine, then put the patient's head in your lap; then heat the cautery so that its form comes out this way after putting a strip of cloth on the tooth; and put the hot cautery inside, and hold it there tightly so that the patient feels the heat coming from the root of the tooth; then release your hand and start again with the cautery according to your will; then fill the patient's mouth with salt water, and let it sit for an hour and rinse it thoroughly.
Et en teil maniere li dens qui estoit movans si est confermez, et li gencive mollifie restrainte, et li moistors corrumpue sechie.	And in this way the tooth that was moving is stabilized, and the gums that were softened are tightened, and the moisture that corrupts is dried up.
de la dolor des dens	of the teeth
Quant dolor de dens vient por froidor, ou il i a froidor ou veir, et les cures de medicine ne valent, adonc i ait mestier de cautere selonc II manieres: et cautere de burre et cautere de feu.	When toothache comes from cold, or if there is coldness or heat, and medicine can't fix it, then you need to use two types of cauterization: butter cauterization and fire cauterization.
Cautere de burre si est telz que tu preignes burre de vaiche, et le bout en une cuillier de fer ou d’arain; aprés pren coton et envolope sus la pointe d’une tente, et la moille en burre bulit, et met sus le dent dolant hastanment et tien tant qu’il soit refroidiez; et ensi fai sovent tant que sa vertus viegne a la racine de la dent, et se tu vues si moille laine et coton en burre froit, et met sus le dent doillant, et met sus I fer chaut tant que li feus viegne au chevement dou dent.	Cautery with butter if it is like that you squeeze butter from a vet's cow, and the tip in a teaspoon of iron or bronze; then take cotton and wrap it over the tip of a tent, and soak it in butter and put it on the tooth sore gently and hold it until it has cooled down; and do this often as long as its virtues come to the root of the tooth, and if you see if that wet wool and cotton in butter freeze, and put it on the sore tooth, and put a hot iron onto it until the fire comes out at the root of the tooth.
Li cauteres ensamble feu si est telz que tu preignes uns cainne de fer ou d’arain, et soit grosse si que li feus ne viegne a la bouche dou malaide; aprés chaufe le cautere, de coi li forme venra ci aprés, et le met sus le dent et tien ta main tant que li cauteres soit refroidiez; fai ceu sovent, car li dolor sera ostee celui jor meisme ou l’endemain.	If the fire cautery is like that you squeeze a iron or bronze wire with your hands, and it is thick so that the fire does not come to the mouth of the sick person; then heat the cautery, for it will take its shape afterward, and put it on the tooth and hold your hand until the cautery has cooled down; do this often, because the pain will be sharp that day or the day after.
Et covient que li malaides emplisse sa bouche de boin burre en l’empressement de cel cautere, et puis le raiche fuer; et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And it is necessary that the sick person fill his mouth with good butter when he applies this cautery, and then remove it; and this is the form of the cautery:
Et fai cautere dou queil chief que tu voudras, et selonc ceu que tu as pooir; et c’est li forme de la caine:	And make the cautery from that part of the mouth which you will, and according to what you can do; and this is the form of the cane:
des scrophules	from scrofula
Quant les scrophules sont de fleume et de moistors froides, et ne sont obeissans a digestion par medicines, adonques eschaufe le cautere cheveit de coi ci aprés vient li forme, et ait II aovertures por les fumees a issir au cautere de l’autre partie; et met le cautere chaut sus l’apostume une fois, ou II se mestier est, tant qu’il viegne au font de l’apostume; et se li apostume est petis si met cautere selonc la quantiteit de l’apostume, et le laisse ensi III jors; et met sus coton moilliet em burre tant que li arsure soit ostee; aprés cure le leu d’oignemens et de tentes tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the scrofula is of cold wet pus, and does not submit to digestion with medicines, then heat the head of the cane so that it comes next: and having made two openings for the fumes to come out from the other side of the cane; put the cane hot on the abscess once, where it is needed, until it reaches the bottom of the abscess; and if the abscess is small, make the cane according to the quantity of the abscess, and leave it there for three days; and put cotton wet with butter on it until the burning is over; then treat the wound with oil and ointment until it is healed.
Li forme de la cainne:	The form of the cane:
Quant les moistors vainquent sus les chenals dou pormon, et meismement quant ce vient de froide complexion, adonc covient que li malaides soit voidiez premiers par medicines solutives; aprés li fai cautere a la racine de la gorge, et te garde que tu ne venir mie jusc’a la gorge, et n’ardre dou keur mais c’un poc.	When the moisture conquers the cheeks of the pommel, and especially when it comes from a cold complexion, then the patient should be voided first by soluable medicines; then make cauterization at the root of the throat, and guard you to not come up to the throat, and dare only a little.
Aprés li fai I autre cautere a la jointure dou col au chief de l’espinee, et soit li cauteres qui est apelez «clavile» de coi nos avons la forme devant; et cure le leu si com nos avons devant dit tant qu’il soit sanez.	After that, make another cauterization at the joint of the neck to the head of the spine, and let be the cauterization which is called 'clavicle', so that we have the form before; and heal the place as we have said before until it is healthy.
de la toust	of the toast
Quant tous et maladie de pormon sont de moistors froides, et li malaides nen ait fievre ne sechor, et est li maladie anciaine, se li fai ij cauteres sus la forcele en leus vuis; et I autre cautere emmi le pis entre II mameles; et soit li cauteres qui est apelez «clavile» selonc la forme qui est devant dite.	When all the disease is of cold moisture, and the patient has no fever or chills, and it is an old disease, then make ij cauterizations on the forelock between the eyebrows; and another cauterization milks between the nipples; and be the cauterizations which are called 'clavicle' according to the form which is before said.
Et se tu vues, fai cautere en poignant a tot le cautere qui est apelez «poins» de coi li forme est ci devant en la maladie des oreilles; et soient li poins jusc’a XXX, ou enqui entor.	And if you see, make cauterization by pricking with all the cauterization that is called 'poins' of which the form is as described above in the disease of the ears; and let the points be up to XXX, or so around.
Aprés cure le leu selonc ceu qui est devant dit, et soit li cauteres a III rains selonc ceste forme:	After care according to this which is before said, and let the cauterization be to three rains according to this form:
Et por ceu sont li cautere plus legier, por ceu que tu en fais III a cop.	And because these are lighter cauterizations, because you do them in three at a time.
de la dislocation de l’ajutoire	of the dislocation of the shoulder
Quant li chiés de l’ajutoire est desaloiez par cause de moistor, et on le remet a leu, et il n’i puet demorer ains revient adés et desalue par petit movement qui avient, si com nos avons esproveit, adonques covient il que tu ramoinnes la dislocation premierement.	When the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have experienced, then you must first reset the dislocation.
Aprés soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos et sus son costeit; aprés lieve le keur qui est dedens le titillite as dois de ta main senestre; et se li jointure est desaluee dedens, si eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners douqueil ci est li forme:	After, let the patient lie on his back and on his left side; after, touch with your right hand the joint that is inside the ear; and if the joint has dislocated inside, then heat the cauterization that is at two dimes in this form:
et cauterize lou keur tant qu’il le perce jusc’a costeit, et venrait li fugure dou cautere ensamble IIII cauteres; et por ceu est faite cautere avec le cautere qui a III ners, por coi li figure de cauterization sunt sis cauteres; et sont li nerf selonc la subtiliteit d’une tente et c’est li forme dou cautere qui a III ners:	and cauterize him until he pierces to the coast, and comes together with the figure of the cautery four cauteries; and for this reason is made cauterization with the cautery that has three nerves, because the figure of the cauterization are there four cauteries; and these nerves according to the subtility of a tent and it is the form of the cautery which has three nerves:
Et aucune fois est ajostez sus ce I nerf por coi il i a VIII cauteres.	And no time is placed on this nerve because there are eight cauteries.
Aprés met sus le cautere porrelz broiez avec seil; aprés fai reposer le malaide, et ne soit meus li membres par lonc tens tant qu’il soit bien confortez.	After it is placed on the cautery, grind it with salt; then let the patient rest, and do not move his members for a long time until he is well comforted.
Et s’il est desaloiez desus, liquelz chose avient poc, adonques fait cautere sus l’epaisse dou cautere clavile, ou mout de cauteres en poignant.	And if it is dislocated above, what thing comes out, then do cauterization on the thick part of the cautery, or many cauteries pierce it.
Car li jointure est refermee, et est ostee li moistor et est sanez li malaides.	And because the joint is closed, and the moisture is dried up and the patient is healed.
Quant en l’estomac vienent froidures et mout de moistors tant qu’il l’estraient a sa complexion, et sont multipliet li catharre a lui, et es manieres de cures acostumees et il ne profite mie, adonc covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son dos, et estende ses jambes et ses mains.	When in the stomach come coldness and moisture as it is drawn away from its color, and multiplies the cataracts to him, and is mannered in the usual cures and does not benefit, then the patient should be placed on his back, and his legs and hands extended.
De ceu en aprés li fai III cauteres I desoz la cuillier dou pis per la quantiteit d’un doi, a tout le cautere clavile, et II cauteres defuers les II costez tant que li figure des cauteres soit a III angles, et ait teil espaice entre l’une et l’autre qu’elles ne soient jointes ensamble quant elles giteront porriture; et soient li cautere si parfont qu’il porpreignent les II pars dou keur, et soit li figure des cauteres selonc ceste forme sens ajostement:	Then after him do three cauterizations of the flesh with the knife, according to the quantity of a two-thirds; all the cauterizations are clawed, and two cauterizations on each side as long as the shape of the cauterizations is at three angles, and there is a space between them that they are not joined together when they go around fire; and that the cauterization is so complete that it burns both sides, and the shape of the cauterizations according to this form without arrangement:
Et se tu vues cauterize d’un grant cautere enmi l’estomac selonc ceste forme; et celui qui avra paour de cest cautere, cauterize en poignant et seigne sus l’estomac i. point selonc la quantiteit que tu vues d’enche; puis le cauterize a tot le cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if you want to cauterize the stomach with a large cauldron according to this form; and he who is afraid of this cauldron, cauterize by stabbing and signing on the stomach at i. point according to the quantity that you see suitable for an ear; then cauterize at all the cauldron called "poins".
Aprés le cure de la cure que nos avons eut devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the treatment of the cure we have had before, as long as he is healthy.
Quant au foie vient dolor de froit et de moistor et de grosse ventositeit, tant qu’il est fuer mis de sa complexion natureil per les superfluitez; et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne li profite mie, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son haitereil; et signe d’enche III cauteres selonc ceste forme et ceste figure et ceste quantiteit sus lou foie, defuer les ypocondres, lai ou li coutes de l’ome vient; et ait d’espaice entre chaicun cautere la groissece d’un doi; et soient li cautere dou lonc dou cors, et ne presser mie mout ta main a tot le cautere; et soit arse tant soulement li moitiez dou keur, et soit li malaides drois sus ses piez; et s’il ne peut, si soit gisans, et estende ses jambes, et lieve ses brais; et c’est li forme:	Regarding the liver, when pain from cold and moisture and strong wind comes, as long as it is freed from its natural substance by excesses; and the patient is treated for what we have said in divisions, and he does not benefit from it unless the patient is reluctant on his back; and sign with an ear III cauterize according to this form and figure and quantity on the liver, leaving space of a thumb between each cauterize; and let the cauterize of the long neck of the torso, and do not press much your hand to all cauterize; and let it be burned so much that half of the cauterize is scorched, and let the patient be laid on his back; and if he cannot, then let him spread his legs, and raise his feet; and this is the form:
Et se ta volentez est, si cauterize ces cauteres dou cutellaire, se tu es subtilz et saiges en l’art, et te warde que tu n’ardes mie tout le keur, car tu feroies sechier tout le cors; et qu’il ne viegne jusc’a boueil, car li keurs est mout subtilz lai endroit, et lou saiches por voir.	Et s'il veut, si cautérise ces cautères du cutelé, s'il est subtil et sage en l'art, et s'il se garde que tu n'ardes tout le corps, car il ferait sécher tout le cours; et qu'il ne vienne jadis jusqu'à la bouillie, car le coup est bien subtil à cet endroit, et le saige pour le voir.
Quant il a apostume au foie, et tu vues savoir s’il est en la char dou foie ou en la toile: s’il est en la char, se sent li malaides dolor ne mie trop fort; et s’il est en la toile, si sent dolor forsenee.	If it has an abscess in the liver, and you can tell whether it is in the parenchyma of the liver or in the capsule: if it is in the parenchyma, then feel that the pain is not too great; but if it is in the capsule, then feel intense pain.
Et lors quant ceste cure desoit les mires, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus sa teste; et puis seigne d’enche le leu ou li apostumes est, et puis chaufe le cautere qui est semblans au rais, de coi ci est li forme:	And when this cure has finished with the boils, then it is necessary that the patient be careful about his head; and then indicate the place where the abscess is, and then heat the fire that resembles a raisin, from which comes the shape:
Et cauterize I cautere tant que li keurs soit ars, et viegne jusc’a syphac, tant que li porreture soit toute fuers; aprés la cure selonc la cure des essues tant qu’il soit sanez; et ne covient mie que de cest cautere use nuls fuers que cil qui ait estudieit longement en l’art de medicine, et par cui mains cestes maladies ont corrut aucune fois.	Et cauterize I cautere tant que li keurs soit ars, et viegne jusc’a syphac, tant que li porreture soit toute fuers; aprés la cure selonc la cure des essues tant qu’il soit sanez; et ne covient mie que de cet cautere use nuls fuers que cil qui ait estudié longement en l'art de médecine, et par cui maints ces maladies ont corrompu aucune fois.
Adonques puet il hardiement ovrer, et toutevoies il me semble que mues vaut li laissier.	And cauterize I cauterize until the wound is burned, and comes up to syphac, until the scar is completely healed; after the cure according to the cure of the abscesses until it is healthy; and only one who has studied long in the art of medicine, and by which many diseases have been corrupted no time.
dou cautere de pleuresin	For the pleurisy cautery
Li ancien dirent que on doit faire a pleuresin cauteres de racines d’aristologe, et en teil maniere: pren une racine d’aristologe longe, la plus grant que tu poras troveir, et soit seche, et soit ausi grosse et ausi longe comme tes dois; et la moille en oile, et l’emprens au feu, et cauterize I cautere entre la forcele et lou col, et II petis cauteres un poc en dessendant en la partie qui est desoz la barbe; et II cauteres entre la quinte coste et la sisime, en declinant derrier un poc; et I cautere emmi le pis, et I autre sus l’estomac, et I entre II espaules, et II as II costez dou pis defuers le cautere qui est entre II espaules; et ne presser mie ta main, ains fai apertement ausi com en odorant.	For the pleurisy cautery. The ancients said that one must do for pleurisy cauterization with roots of aristorlogia, and in this way: take a root of aristorlogia long, the greatest that you can find, and let it dry, and also be as thick and as long as your two hands; and soak it in oil, and hold it to the fire, and cauterize I cauterize between the rib and the collarbone, and II small cauterizations a little down going down into the part that is desoz the beard; and cauterize between the fifth rib and the sixth, declining behind a little; and I cauterize emmi the pis, and I another sus the stomach, and I between the two shoulders, and II the costez dou pis defuers the cautere who is between the two shoulders; and do not press your hand, otherwise open it as if you were smelling it.
Et dirent aucun ancien que aucun home usent de cautere de feir semblant a I raseur, et l’eschaufent et le mettent entre les costes, tant qu’il vient a cel aposteme; et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	And no old man used fire cautery like a razor, and scoured it and put it between the ribs until it reached the abscess; and withered away the pain, as we have said in the incision of the liver.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this work there is fear or the patient dies now, or a fistula comes out that cannot be cured.
de la mice	of the mouse
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent III manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When you cure the disease of the mouse according to what we have said in the division of the cures, and it does not benefit, then they took three ways of cauterizing which are all good.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant; et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos; et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule; et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	Of these three ways, one is that you make three cauterizations, or four, according to the length of the mouse, according to the shape of the fire cautery of the liver which we have said before; and do not press your hand all the way along the cauterization, and let the patient sweat on his back; and another way of cauterizing is that you scurry the cauterizer which has two edges, as we have demonstrated in the dislocation of the shoulder; and apply the fire to the place of the mouse, where the cut comes towards the left, and let the elevation which you feel by the fire be according to the length, and the cauterization is according to the width of the chest.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	After placing the fire on both sides until the heat is felt through the bottom, then remove and let it cool down for a few hours. And if you see that, cauterize with all three, and if you don't see anything, cauterize with just two.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the patient has been infected for a long time, and it is clear that one of the two cures mentioned earlier is needed, then it is necessary to try both at the same time.
de ydropisie	dropies
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	 cautery does not work for droves, except in the way called "asclepiades".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis; et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	When you apply the cure as we have described in the divisions, and your cure does not benefit, then it is necessary that you make four cauteries around the body, and one on the stomach, and one on the liver, and one on the back of the neck, and one under the armpit; and let the cauteries be close to the spine of the patient.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere; et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	After leaving the fire cautery in place for a long time, do not abandon the treatment of the patient after the cauterization; and healing would be hastened, and both intentions would be accomplished with the help of God.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit; et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	The shape of the cautery for the abdomen is a key that we have in front of us; and what is for the back is olive-shaped, according to what has been said before.
de l’enfleure des piez	of swelling of the parts
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	When the parts are swollen in the person who is gouty, and they are pale yellow, you must cauterize on the back of the foot between the index and middle fingers; and lift your hand away from the cautery without turning it.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply, lest the pale yellow be burned, and let the cauterization be according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After that, do the same on the other leg at the tip of the cut; and let the cautery be long, one over the knee cap and the other behind, under the leg; and leave the cauteries in place for a long time without treating, because they will hurt themselves; after that, treat the rest as said above.
de la menoison	of the house
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	When the solution of the abdomen comes from cold and moisture, as long as the virtues that retain and digest it remain in the stomach and in the intestines are affrayed, and cannot be cured by any means of treatment; and you will see the patient very suffering and of great virtue, so make a large cautery on the stomach according to what he has spoken about before or the cautery of the stomach, flowing around; and four cauteries around the navel very finely, two on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see moisture abundant and the patient suffering, then make fire cautery on the knuckle, and I make cautery on each finger, and II small cauterizes in the stomach to take away the great one, for the cure is profitable when there is good help.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	When the hemorrhoids are at the foundation, or one or more, and are old and are large cold and moist corrupted humors, and are cured as we have said in the divisions, and it does not profit, then make fire cautery: III on the spine of the back, that which is all farther from the buttocks little by little and in triangling, and I cauterize them two times; and if you think that the stomach is cold, and the meat does not cook, and a swelling appears on the face, then the face I make a large cautery on the stomach, as it is said before, and another one on the liver, and another one on the cheek at all cauterize key; and leave the cautery open for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After care, let him rest as long as he is healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the charred flesh which is called "thela
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit; et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort; fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit; aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez; et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	When you cope to the charred flesh, if you heat the cautery which seems like a razor, and then put it all ablaze on the coped flesh; and leave as much as your hand so that the cauterization comes to the birth of the vein, from which it is free; do this once or twice, and if there is much charred flesh, cauterize each one as we have said; after the application of beneficial ointments as long as they are healthy; and if you cauterize with a large cautery on the alchatim, it will be more helpful.
de plaie mal curee	of a wound badly treated
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot bear to have the wound lanced or opened, which we will tell you in your place, then comes a disease that cannot be healed except by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When there is no outlet for the blood, and it has risen and become thick with pus and moisture, then you must try to provide a small passage for it, and be careful that you know how much of the remedy is perfect.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	After warming the fire that seems like a razor, and pouring it into the fistula according to the quantity by which the remedy has entered, and restarting the fire as often as the course of pus and corrosion is burned, once or three times, according to the amount of treatment required; and be careful not to hurt the nerves that are in there, and great veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	If the fistula goes to the chest of the belly and intestine, be careful of these veins, and do not make them except in their charnel, and think that they are not persistant; after treating the vein as long as it is healthy, and if the veins have been broken, and the matter has been exposed for a long time, then know that the vein is completely healthy; and if the matter has not been exposed, know that the veins are three and rotten at their ends; and thus, as one of these that we will say in its place.
de la maladie des reins	of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit; et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	When the pain of the kidneys comes with great windiness and does not respond to treatment by a woman, then it is necessary that you make a fire cautery on both sides of the kidneys with the claw-shaped cautery which we have mentioned above; and if we make them in the middle, there will be three cauterizations in line, and they will do more good.

de la marris	of the urinary tract.
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	When the urethra is cold and moist, so that it does not allow conception, and the flowers are corrupted and their termini are delayed; and when they come, there is great pain: then it is necessary that one make three cauterizations around the bouge, as we have said above for the cauterization of the bladder, and two cauterizations behind the back; and let the cauterizations be with the claw-shaped cautery, as we have said.
de la hainche	of the hip
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When the viscous moisture goes down into the box of the hip, and for this reason it moves from its place, and the sign is that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together; and the places of the department are found out, so that you cauterize the patient on the hip box with the fire-cautery in a circle shape, and sign before the place around the box like it comes back, so that the box is inside the circle; and if it is such as those that have been cauterized in the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If this cauterization has not been performed for you, make three cauterizations with the large olive-oil fire, and let the cauterization be perfect as all the others; and treat it until it is cured.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the hip pain
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When pain comes in the hip joint, and it is from cold and moisture, and the patient is cured of what we have said in the division, and the cure does not work, and the disease is old: then you must purging the sick with large humors of pills made rotten, or other bad-looking pills.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	After the fire cautery; and the way of the cautery so is according to II manners: that is to say together burning medicines, and fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Fire cautery is according to many manners, of which one is: that you cauterize over the hip joint three triangular cauters according to this form, and make them deep and wide, and space between each cauter with a diameter of two, and let them be olive-colored; never do you make cauter on top of the head of the hip, for there are four according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you see that the cautery at the ring that we have said before in the dislocation of the hip; but do it in such a way that the ring contains all the hip, and all the flesh of the leg is burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the way it is done in sciatica, when the pain remains in the hip and does not reach up to the thigh or up to the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if the pain only reaches up to the thigh and leg, then two cauterizations are made at the place where the patient feels the pain, one above the ankle and another above the foot, on the left side; and either the cauterization is cutaneous, and the flesh of the leg is burned; and if the patient feels that the pain extends to two or three toes or near them, then cauterize at the place where he feels the pain for three or four points, or at the cautery which is called "poins".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	Et si the surgeon is skilled, he does it more skillfully; and if the patient says that the pain is in the groin towards the thigh, he does a cauterization with a cutting or circular knife, and you must take great care with all your cauterizations so that you do not let go of the cautery as much as the cautery burns the nerves and large arteries, and do not cause great harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I have seen many who have done cauterization on the heel of the foot, and left them so much that the leg was all twisted, and the toes as well, and they were pierced and corrupted all the toes.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a solution to the belly from which he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two parts together, do cauterization in one and the other, according to this way.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	And the sage said in the cauterization of the heel, from which this is the way, do one so and the other too large as a thumb nail, or one less, and be between joints and also between one joint and the other of a space the quantity of a nut; and let the joints be above the two parts, and also be like nails, and there is one made well of iron; and this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	And let it be heated until it is completely red and cool, and then put it on the chest piece of the sick person, and let it turn around under the left rib; and let him cauterize once I cauterization will cure him and leave III days; and then make a plaster of tar, and leave the open wound for a long time; after the cure of ointment until he is well.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	Al-Buqā'īs says that we should use little of this cauterization because of the danger of scorching, and few people use it; but this is a good cauterization, which can bear it, and leave it where it burns.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	The medical cauterization of fire is such that you make a tool to hold between the edges of the opening, and let it be made of brass or iron with a high wall, and there are two points on either side of the size of a double palm; and they open up and down, and join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche; aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After you have lifted the hip bone from the patient lying on his back, and quickly place your hand above it; after that, place between the two circles of hot ash that are heated in the fire a cup, and leave it for an hour, and suffer the patient the heat and burning.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is the same as with fire; and when the mediation has passed, remove your hand from the instrument and raise the hip of soft ash, and leave it for three days, and put on butter as much as the burning black part is healed; and let it be three days until the rot gets out; and that one behind would help after the treatment of ointments until he is well.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument; et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And if the pain extends to the thigh or to the leg, make the instrument that you have made in the hip grow larger; and this is the way of hot ash, and I have written it here in the treatise of medical correction.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkali and live charcoal, as much of one as of the other, and grind them together and put them in a nine-pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	Take some small holes in the bottom of one so that the liquid can flow through; and put this pot on top of another well-plugged pot, and put alkali and charcoal and sweet water on it, as much as you need to fill the two pots up to the tops; and leave it like this until it has drained all the water out and the pot is full of ash; then take all the ash, and put it on top of the charcoal and alkali, just as we have said.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	And then when it is well-dampened and purified with the work of medicine and other cauterizations, for it performs such a work as fire does; and with other medicines which are well-purified in this way, as with perspiration, honey, and charcoal with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galiens tells us of a remedy in which a noble man was cured of the pain in the hip and sciatic leg, and he drank it, and said that another did not cure him, but he was healed in one soul when this remedy was made, and he bathed himself as it is taught hereafter.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie; et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	And he said in this way that you squeeze green fresh and dry alum and grind it with a little fat, and put it on the hip and thigh and leg where the pain is, and let it sit; and leave it for III hours and by the quantity that the patient no longer feels the burning.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then let him enter or bath as long as his body is a little warm, and make him enter the bed, and the pain will go away all and he will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use fire cautery of such medicines, except after the evacuation of blood.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout; et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And Dyescorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with the end of a goat's horn, then it helps much; and this cautery must be made in a certain way.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take another, and oil it well, and put it on the crease that is between the thumb of the foot and the other which is called a flick.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	Afterwards take dry goat's horn, and put it on fire until it becomes coals, and lay it on the wool, and leave it until it is cold; and do this again, and do not cease to do this until you think by sense that it has come up to the knee, and that the pain has ceased; and this way of cauterizing is called "goats horn cautery".
de la dolor dou dos	of the pain at the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, or by sitting down or by pounding, or by too great an evacuation, or by the appearance of expanded cold material, no one of these appearances is worth cauterizing, except that which comes from the infusion of cold material.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor; et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	Often this disease occurs in small children and the signs of onset are that they become stiff when they stand up and are afraid; and you will find in the lower spine at the back and in us the appearance that comes on the others.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this person and you see him healed, if he is cauterized with the cauldron of fire according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	Let the fire cautery each part of the spine evenly.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, then cauterize around the spine with a piercing cautery two or three lines, and let the burns be close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After cure the area until it is healthy according to what we have said, and be careful not to apply cauterization to a ganglion that is in a nerve's spine.
de la dolor des jointes	of the joints' pain
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When the joints' pain is due to moisture that spreads to each limb, and when the pain comes in pieces, which is called "podagre" properly, and when it is caused by cold and cannot be cured with medicine, then cure it with cauterization in this way: Make a cauldron of cauterizing liquid around the joint of the foot, and let the cauterizer be olive-colored according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if it is necessary for you to hold on the face of the foot, make a fire cautery with all the fire cautery that is called "no point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if the pains come up only to the kneecaps and to other joints, and it happens many times, make a fire cautery on each of them III cauterizes or IIII of each part, with all the olive oil cautery; and if you need more, do more, but don't hold your hand hard, only as long as the skin of the knee is burnt.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains go down to the knees and back, administer the cautery that we have spoken about in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pains are in the hands, make a point between the fingers; and if there is still pain in the two bones, make a point on each joint and on the hair of the hand; and if the pains come up to the elbows or shoulders, cauterize each part, and give good advice to the patient and use medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	Because if you do good management and you purify the pus, then you will be healed with the help of God.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rupture of the syrup
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When the rupture comes in anger, and the bouels descend as coions and is new, so that when you see it cured, it does not hurt him that day; and he uses things that leave his belly, so that the end descends from his belly; after he sits down on his back between your hands, and orders him to tie his hair as long as his boils are repaired, and bring them to your hands, and sign with an arch at the top of the chest; then heat the fire with which this is done:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	as long as it is white and it seems solid.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Then bring the boules to their place; and the minister tie his hand so that it does not turn back; and well work on the patient's legs, and put a cussin and a serjant on the legs, and one on the feet that hold the hands; then put the fire on the mark with your whole hand, and keep it straight and keep it until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, start again another time until you touch the bone; and beware carefully that the boules do not escape when you make the fire; so that you do not burn them, and that by this the patient does not die, or some other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you come only to the bone with the fire cautery, your work is worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And it is necessary that the cauterizations of children be subtle according to the measure of their bones, and of the great people also great according to their measure; after three days cure let the place of the cautery of butter be warm until the bone is exposed; after the cure apply other oils until he is well, and lay the patient on his back for 40 days until the wound is well sealed; and it is necessary that his movements be restricted for a long time, so that the blister does not rise when he gets up to go to bed.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	After 40 days, when he wants to get up, a well-made bandage is provided for him, and it is kept for another 40 days; and he should have good rest, so that he works little and guards against too much drinking and eating, and against too loud shouting; and when he follows this teaching, he will be fully healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say hereafter the cure of cutting in his chalk.
de la routure dou ventre	Of the uterine rupture
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	When ruptures come in other wombs and are known, and you see that they no longer grow, make I the cautery of cautery according to its quantity, and let it be burned with fire the third time of the cure; after the cure according to what we have said; and none of the ancients have said that one must cauterize with cautery the three angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but first the sign the place of the navel and make a line through the largeness on the rupture, and another away from it, and all your hand in every cauterized claw.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauterizes are lighter and softer.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of ancient pain in no member
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes in no member, or from sitting or from hurting, and this pain lasts a long time, and the cure of medicine is not useful, then it is necessary that it be cauterized with fire which is called "poins", and make the cauterize according to the length of the member and its smallness and its weakness and its virtue and its location of torments and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If it has healed from the first fire cautery, that is good. But if not, restart the cautery process on top of the previous one, for the custom is that it must grow at the member nearest to it, so you should perform the cauterizations as long as the patient remains unhealed.
de meselerie	from healing
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The meseile are not aided at all by cautery, nor do the diseases arise from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy alone.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	But if not, restart the cautery process on top of the previous one, for the custom is that it must grow at the member nearest to it, so you should perform the cauterizations as long as the patient remains unhealed.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules; et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	And if the sweating is everywhere scattered; and it loses manifestly, so that you have to cauterize this cauteries which we said above, and I cauterize in some place of the neck, and II cauterizes on the spine of the back, and I great cauterizes on the skull, and I another cauterize, and II cauterizes on the shoulders; and II cauterizes on the ribs, and II cauterizes on the loin muscles, and I cauterize on each joint of the hands and feet, and on the grooves of the hands; and beware of the nerves that are behind the legs walking, so that you do not burn them; and never make a cauterization on the bone of the hand, and another on the bone of the stomach, and another on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And know that the more I make a cauterization, the more I do good and profit; and know that the patient does not feel pain at the cauterization as much as the healthy person feels it, because the body is already very corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the cauterization be great or small according to the limbs and joints, according to what you will find in the manner of irons.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After care let him sit with flour of times with honey and other cures as long as he is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When it swells in any member and is cured with medicines and oils and poultices, and is not yet healed, then make the cauterization on the member according to its greatness and smallness; and let the cauterization be a little bit inside the cure of the ointment until he is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	And no time is made to cauterize and by hand and by foot and by back, at the exit of the nerve that silences the member, and in this way if it is osteized; and nevertheless nothing is mixed with him unless he knows the limbs and exits of the moving nerved body.
de albaras	of albaras
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the disease called "albaras" is awake, and the medicine does not help, then cauterize with a fire cautery a little perfectly, according to the quantity of the juice of currants, as long as the blenchour [bleeding] is stopped, and its color changes; then cure with flour of dates and lentils with oil of roses and leaves of plantain, and blood of lamb and blood of pigeon, each a part; and mix them all together, and tie it with a cloth, and apply it to the affected area until it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	the cure for syphilis by cautery
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When the itch begins to appear, and you see it stopping, if you cauterize with a fire cautery that seems like a circle, all around the itch's circumference.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And all ways the sage men say that one should also make a cautery on the middle of the abscess; and to me this does not seem good, because I fear that it may become inflamed and rotten, and I have never wanted to do so before; and the most right thing is that it be cauterized inside, at the cautery which is called "circulating", as we have said in many cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the swelling that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	When anyone has a disease that is called "adebelati", and it lingers until it dies or because of the excess fluid it produces or because of the age of the sick person when he is very old and has little blood, or because of the heat of the sickness: then cauterize it inside with many small cauteries while pricking; then leave it like that.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For she is eager to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you pierce it throughout the whole cautery, let the cautery be very hot.
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And put your hand in the middle of this disease called "adubelati" as long as the cauterization has penetrated the cure, and is such a cauterization that the patient feels the heat in some way that the course of the pus is controlled.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the cure until he is completely healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	the fire cure by iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another kind of disease that is called "corrodens", and is nothing other than a putrid mass of a member, because it corrodes the members as much as the fire dries up the wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	If you see this disease in its early stages that can be cured with fire and claws together, then heat the claws very small and very large according to what is appropriate for the place where the disease is; after cauterizing it on all sides until it is completely corroded, and nothing remains of it, so that whatever is corrupted is taken away.
